msg:This is a super enjoyable weekend trip to Wuyi Mountain. The hotel is hidden in a tea house as mentioned before on the Internet. Not only the beautiful environment, but also its own tea mountain, tea room, tea factory and tea museum, away from the hustle and bustle of the city, you can completely relax here. The hotel's service was warm and thoughtful. They arranged pick-up and drop-off from the high-speed rail station and sent us to the pier to ride rafting on Jiuqu River. They also extended our check-out time so that we could have time to return to the hotel to take a shower after climbing the mountain the next day. rest. The hotel's restaurant has a rich variety of dishes, both breakfast and lunch, and the taste is excellent. Special thanks to the manager, Ms. Ye Dan, for her warm reception, which made our weekend in Wuyishan particularly enjoyable. It is highly recommended that guests visiting Wuyi Mountain stay at this hotel!
